<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рулевой.html>рулево́й</a> (28636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руль.html>руль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rulʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рулевой.html>рулево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rulevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> steering, rudder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рулевой.html>рулево́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:колесо.html>колесо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rulevóje</b> kolesó</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>steering</b> wheel</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>helmsman</li></ol>

***рулить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рулить.html>рули́ть</a> (23907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руль.html>руль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rulʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рулить.html>рули́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rulítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to taxi</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steer the wheel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be in charge, to be in the driver's seat</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:румяный.html>румя́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rumjána</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:румянец.html>румя́нец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rumjánec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:румянец.html>румя́нца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:румянец.html>румя́нцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:румянец.html>румя́нцев</a></b>)

***румяный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:румяный.html>румя́ный</a> (6083)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">румꙗнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rumjanŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ruměnъ</i>, from earlier <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rudměnъ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁rewdʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:румяный.html>румя́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rumjányj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ruddy, rosy, pink</li></ol>

***русский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>русский</a> (1605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">русьскъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rusĭskŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русь.html>Русь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Rusʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Rus</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span>, <span class="ann-pos">adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rússkij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Russian
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rússkaja</b> vódka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Russian</b> vodka</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сская</a></b> вы́хухоль</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rússkaja</b> výxuxolʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Desmana_moschata" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Desmana moschata"><i>Desmana moschata</i></a></span>) <b>Russian</b> desman, <b>Russian</b> muskrat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rússkij</b> zamók</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Russian</b> lock, Sklifosovsky’s lock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:осетр.html>осётр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rússkij</b> osjótr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Acipenser_gueldenstaedtii" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Acipenser gueldenstaedtii"><i>Acipenser gueldenstaedtii</i></a></span>) <b>Russian</b> sturgeon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́з</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rússkij</b> moróz</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Russian</b> frost <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">very cold weather</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></b> «<a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сь</a>»</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">said about the alleged unconcern of Russians and their tendency to rely on luck</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rússkij</b> “avósʹ”</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Russian</b> serendipity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:балет.html>бале́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rússkij</b> balét</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Russian</b> ballet</span></div></dd>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rússkij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сского</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сские</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сских</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сская</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Russian, an ethnic Russian person (for Russian national or resident, see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:россиянин.html>россия́нин</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rossijánin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>ведь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vy vedʹ <b>rússkij</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You’re Russian, aren’t you?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> та́к-ли?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vy <b>rússkij</b>, ne ták-li?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You’re Russian, aren’t you?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the Russian language (short for <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rússkij jazýk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ешь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty znáješʹ <b>rússkij</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you know Russian?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Do not confuse the noun or adjective <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rússkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:российский.html>росси́йский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rossíjskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:россиянин.html>россия́нин</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rossijánin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, both of which translate to Russian.
</p>
<dl><dd>The word <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rússkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, concerning a person or people, means pertaining to ethnic East Slavic Russians only, but not to other ethnic groups in Russia.</dd>
<dd>The word <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:российский.html>росси́йский</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rossíjskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means pertaining to the state or nation of Russia.</dd></dl>

***русый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:русый.html>ру́сый</a> (7409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">русъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rusŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rusъ</i>, from earlier <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rudsъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁rowdʰ-s-o-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русый.html>ру́сый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rúsyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fair(-haired), blond(e), light brown (of hair), dirty blond</li></ol>

***рухнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рухнуть.html>ру́хнуть</a> (2730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рухнуть.html>ру́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rúxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушиться.html>ру́шиться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to collapse, to crash</li>
<li>to fall through, to crash, to fail
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жды</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рухнуть.html>ру́хнули</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одночасье.html>одноча́сье</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vse moí nadéždy <b>rúxnuli</b> v odnočásʹje.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">All my hopes crashed overnight.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ручаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́ться</a> (8977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ручи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ručítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ručátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поручиться.html>поручи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to warrant, to guarantee, to certify, to answer for, to vouch for <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, someone/something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́юсь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>ručájusʹ</b> za éto golovój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'll <b>answer/vouch</b> for it with my life; I'll stake my life on it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́юсь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> ....</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ručájusʹ</b> za to, što ....</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>guarantee</b> that ....</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́юсь</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja za sebjá ne <b>ručájusʹ</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't <b>guarantee</b> I'll control myself.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to assure, to promise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́юсь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> ....</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ručájusʹ</b> tebé, što ....</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I assure you that ...</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́юсь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лаю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ručájusʹ</b>, što sdélaju éto.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I promise I will do it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bet, to be sure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́юсь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> ...</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ručájusʹ</b>, što ...</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>bet</b> (that) ...; I <b>am sure</b> (that) ...</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ручаться.html>руча́юсь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ručájusʹ</b>, što vam étovo ne sdélatʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I bet you can't do that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ručajь</i>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ruká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручка.html>ру́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rúčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручка.html>ру́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручка.html>ру́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручка.html>ру́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ruká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: small hand</li>
<li>handle, crank</li>
<li>knob</li>
<li>grip</li>
<li>chair arm</li>
<li>lever</li>
<li>pen, fountain pen</li>
<li>pen holder</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ручной.html>ручно́й</a> (4680)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ruká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ручной.html>ручно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ručnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hand; manual
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ручной.html>ручна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кладь.html>кладь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ručnája</b> kladʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>hand</b> luggage</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>handmade</li>
<li>tame, domesticated</li></ol>

***рушащийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рушащийся.html>ру́шащийся</a> (9629)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***рушить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рушить.html>ру́шить</a> (17812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рꙋшити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rušiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to destroy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ру́шити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rúšyty</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move, to wiggle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">руша́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rušáty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">ру́шыць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rúšycʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move, to wiggle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">роушити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rušiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to destroy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушить.html>ру́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rúša</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to destroy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ру̏шити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to destroy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">rúšiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shake, to demolish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">rȗšim</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">rušit</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to disturb, to break the silence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">rušiť</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">ruszyć</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">rušowaś</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rage, to make noise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>More distantly cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">raũsti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">rausiù</i>, 1sg. past <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">rausiaũ</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">ràust</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rake, to sweep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">ràušu</i>, 1sg. past <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">ràusu</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">rausis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">rūsỹs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cellar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">rū́sas</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">ruzga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fidgety person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">rušinât</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">rusums</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">steep bank</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span mention" lang="non">rúst</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ruin, ruined wall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">ryskja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушить.html>ру́шить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rúšitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to raze, to tear down</li>
<li>to husk (grain)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рушник.html>рушни́к</a> (27162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушник.html>рушни́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rušník</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушник.html>рушника́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушник.html>рушники́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушник.html>рушнико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarus" class="extiw" title="w:Belarus">Belarus</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukraine" class="extiw" title="w:Ukraine">Ukraine</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> towel</li>
<li>rushnyk, rushnik, ruchnik <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">traditional embroidered towel or cloth</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***рыба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́ба</a> (983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ryba</i>, akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rīpārius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of a riverbank</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> inhabiting the river.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́ба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rýba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́бы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>рыб</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fish <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">as a living animal</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fish <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">as food</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушеный.html>сушёная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́ба</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sušónaja <b>rýba</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">dried <b>fish</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dominoes</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blocked game; block</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> publishing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> placeholder, lorem ipsum</li></ol>
